 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle">


<IMG SRC="g910027g0130064932372.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Suspends Quarterly Dividend as Company Continues Disciplined Execution </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Against Strategic Priorities </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD,
Ill., Jan. 30, 2025 &#150; Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA) today announced that its board of directors is suspending the company&#146;s cash dividend historically paid to stockholders on a quarterly basis, as management continues to
evaluate and refine its capital allocation policy consistent with the company&#146;s broader long-term turnaround efforts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This change in capital
allocation is aimed at strengthening WBA&#146;s balance sheet by reducing debt over time and improving free cash flow, as the company works toward achieving a retail <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pharmacy-led</FONT> turnaround underpinned by a
sustainable economic model. The company&#146;s cash needs over the next several years, including with respect to litigation and debt refinancing, were important considerations as part of the decision to suspend the dividend. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA leadership remains focused on successfully executing against its strategic priorities and maintaining financial discipline, which it believes will deliver
sustained value creation over the long term. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance (Nasdaq: WBA) is an integrated healthcare, pharmacy and retail leader serving millions of customers and patients every day, with a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">175-year</FONT> heritage of caring for communities. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A trusted, global innovator in retail pharmacy with approximately 12,500
locations across the U.S., Europe and Latin America, WBA plays a critical role in the healthcare ecosystem. Through dispensing medicines, improving access to pharmacy and health services, providing high quality health and beauty products and
offering anytime, anywhere convenience across its digital platforms, WBA is shaping the future of healthcare in the thousands of communities it serves and beyond. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA employs approximately 312,000 people, with a presence in eight countries and consumer brands including: Walgreens, Boots, Duane Reade, the No7 Beauty
Company and Benavides.<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP>The Company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. In fiscal 2024, WBA scored 100% on
the Disability Equality Index for disability inclusion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More Company information is available at <U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Cautionary Note Regarding Forward-Looking Statements: All statements in this press release that are not historical, including statements regarding
WBA&#146;s broader turnaround efforts and refining its capital allocation, generating positive cash flows and strengthening WBA&#146;s balance sheet, the ability of WBA to pay dividends in the future, achieving a sustainable economic model,
executing against strategic priorities and delivering sustained value creation over the long term, are forward-looking statements for </I></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="right">


<IMG SRC="g910027g0130064932642.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. | walgreensbootsalliance.com </P>

</DIV></Center>
